<div id="review_229912915" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/229912915" />
    <a title="Arlene" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1746727-arlene"><img alt="Arlene" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1347048609p2/1746727.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/229912915?book_show_action=true">Nov 01, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Arlene" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Arlene" href="/user/show/1746727-arlene">Arlene</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=read-2015">read-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=overdrive-audio">overdrive-audio</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer229912915" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11965791648173659321"><b>Full of Spoilers – Proceed with caution.</b><br/><br/>The Rise of Nine is explosive, adrenaline pumping and full of high power energy. I expected nothing less with this installment. <br/><br/>In this installment, Number Six, Seven and Ten go in search of Eight and they find him in India. Across the world, Four and Nine are traveling together and Five is still missing. Setrakus Ra is on earth and invading Four and Eight’s mind through dreams and visions. The Government is working with the Mogadorians for the benefit of </span>
  <span id="freeText11965791648173659321" style="display:none"><b>Full of Spoilers – Proceed with caution.</b><br /><br />The Rise of Nine is explosive, adrenaline pumping and full of high power energy. I expected nothing less with this installment. <br /><br />In this installment, Number Six, Seven and Ten go in search of Eight and they find him in India. Across the world, Four and Nine are traveling together and Five is still missing. Setrakus Ra is on earth and invading Four and Eight’s mind through dreams and visions. The Government is working with the Mogadorians for the benefit of rare minerals, weapons and finding other life sustaining planets.<br /><br />So much happened during this installment that it was like a constant action-packed film with no downtime, which I loved! <br /><br />In this book, it was clear that Four is distracted by Sarah and Sam. He wants to find them and keep them safe, and luckily they do find Sarah, and she redeems herself for what she did in the previous book. However Four needs to refocus on his mission of saving Lorien and keeping the Garde together. <br /><br />We got to know Nine a little bit better and I really liked his character. Nine is hard-edge and reckless probably because he was tortured by the Mogs for over a year, so he’s consumed with revenge. Nine needs to harnesss his revenge, learn to work with his Garde, and refocus his energy in a more controlled manner.<br /><br />As with the first two books, Six remains my favorite. She’s badass, headstrong, determined and fierce. I see her as a leader alongside Four in this mission.<br /><br />The last chapters end in an epic battle with Setrakus Ra and at the end, the Garde knows they need to train and strategize together in order to win this war. The Lorien Garde are a force to be reckoned with! Looking forward to the next installment.<br /><br /><b>Members of the Garde</b><br />Number Four: Resistant to fire, telekinesis, lumen. New – Healing power and more complex lumen power. Possibly Piticus Lore’s abilities.<br />Number Five: Still missing.<br />Number Six: Invisibility, telekinesis, change weather<br />Number Seven: Breathe under water, telekinesis, can undo damage inflicted on those who don’t deserve it, heals others and herself, nocturnal vision. New – can move trees and landscape.<br />Number Eight: Found in this series. Turns into an animal, tele-transport, telekinesis, images of the future<br />Number Nine: Xray vision, antigravity, superior hearing, can transfer powers<br />Number Ten: Ella – Can change her age, telepathy. Is still developing her legacies.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11965791648173659321" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('gT4AJ0NmRXJ3uBr3KE5FOH4ci9Md2hnntA7XzAhO7DW7GGn1+DiMGtCTrpbfu0/nqENsG9NXl4DvcJF9xQ0erw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('3pDuyEAhBFSuO29dLVtlLfXltJKb7cubJFNZtMi0Kjrktoca+3/NPAkQ2zzarm/yI7pTWlVgRfx/LR8FBffYoA==')})
  }
